List of All Known Arcades and Amusement Operators
as of January 1, 1991
In our continuing effort to provide you with historical information for the amusement industry, here is a list of all known arcades and amusement operators as of January, 1991.

This is a combined list, the only way I have it available. It is arranged in zip code order and was designed as a mailing list for the industry.

Most of the arcades were personally visited during the period from 1986-1988 in the following states: Florida, Georgia, Kentucky, Mississippi, New Jersey, New York, Pennsylvania, Texas. This includes ALL known locations as of the time the trip was made in the state (included all sparsely populated areas).
